```typescript
/**
 * WebSocketManager tests
 */

import { WebSocketManager, WebSocketState } from '../../../src/utils/websocket';
import { WebSocketError, TimeoutError } from '../../../src/utils/errors';

// Mock WebSocket
class MockWebSocket {
  public static CONNECTING = 0;
  public static OPEN = 1;
  public static CLOSING = 2;
  public static CLOSED = 3;

  public readyState = MockWebSocket.CONNECTING;
  public onopen: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onmessage: ((event: MessageEvent) => void) | null = null;
  public onerror: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onclose: ((event: CloseEvent) => void) | null = null;

  constructor(
    public url: string,
    public protocols?: string | string[]
  ) {}

  send = jest.fn();
  close = jest.fn((code?: number, reason?: string) => {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(
        new CloseEvent('close', {
          code: code ?? 1000,
          reason: reason ?? '',
        }) as any
      );
    }
  });

  // Test helpers
  triggerOpen() {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.OPEN;
    if (this.onopen) {
      this.onopen(new Event('open'));
    }
  }

  triggerMessage(data: string) {
    if (this.onmessage) {
      this.onmessage(new MessageEvent('message', { data }));
    }
  }

  triggerError() {
    if (this.onerror) {
      this.onerror(new Event('error'));
    }
  }

  triggerClose(code = 1000, reason = '') {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(new CloseEvent('close', { code, reason }) as any);
    }
  }
}

describe('WebSocketManager', () => {
  let manager: WebSocketManager;
  let mockWs: MockWebSocket;

  beforeEach(() => {
    // Mock global WebSocket
    (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
      mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
      // Automatically trigger open after a microtask to simulate async connection
      Promise.resolve().then(() => {
        if (mockWs.readyState === MockWebSocket.CONNECTING) {
          mockWs.triggerOpen();
        }
      });
      return mockWs;
    });

    manager = new WebSocketManager({
      url: 'wss://test.example.com',
      connectionTimeout: 1000,
    });
  });

  afterEach(() => {
    jest.clearAllMocks();
  });

  describe('initialization', () => {
    it('should create manager with options', () => {
      expect(manager).toBeInstanceOf(WebSocketManager);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should not be connected initially', () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('connection', () => {
    it('should connect to WebSocket', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);
    });

    it('should create WebSocket with correct URL', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(mockWs.url).toBe('wss://test.example.com');
    });

    it('should pass protocols to WebSocket', async () => {
      const managerWithProtocols = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        protocols: ['protocol1', 'protocol2'],
      });

      await managerWithProtocols.connect();

      expect(mockWs.protocols).toEqual(['protocol1', 'protocol2']);
    });

    it('should timeout if connection takes too long', async () => {
      const shortTimeoutManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        connectionTimeout: 100,
      });

      await expect(shortTimeoutManager.connect()).rejects.toThrow(TimeoutError);
    });

    it('should not connect twice', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      const wsConstructorCalls = ((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length;

      await manager.connect();

      expect(((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length).toBe(wsConstructorCalls);
    });

    it('should handle connection errors', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerError();
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Connection failed');

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe('message handling', () => {
    it('should receive messages through handler', async () => {
      const messageHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: messageHandler,
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test message');

      expect(messageHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          data: 'test message',
        })
      );
    });

    it('should handle multiple messages', async () => {
      const messages: string[] = [];

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: (event) => messages.push(event.data),
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('message1');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message2');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message3');

      expect(messages).toEqual(['message1', 'message2', 'message3']);
    });
  });

  describe('sending data', () => {
    it('should send string data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      manager.send('test data');

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith('test data');
    });

    it('should send ArrayBuffer data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(8);
      manager.send(buffer);

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith(buffer);
    });

    it('should throw error when sending while disconnected', () => {
      expect(() => manager.send('test')).toThrow(WebSocketError);
    });
  });

  describe('disconnection', () => {
    it('should disconnect gracefully', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should disconnect with custom code and reason', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect(1001, 'Going away');

      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith(1001, 'Going away');
    });

    it('should handle disconnect when not connected', async () => {
      await expect(manager.disconnect()).resolves.not.toThrow();
    });

    it('should timeout disconnect if it takes too long', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Override close to not trigger event
      mockWs.close = jest.fn();

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();

      // Should resolve after timeout
      await expect(disconnectPromise).resolves.not.toThrow();
    }, 10000);
  });

  describe('reconnection', () => {
    it('should attempt reconnection on unexpected close', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      // Simulate unexpected close
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Abnormal closure');

      // Wait for reconnection attempt
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.RECONNECTING);
    });

    it('should not reconnect if disabled', async () => {
      const noReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: { enabled: false },
      });

      const connectPromise = noReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(noReconnectManager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should stop reconnecting after max attempts', async () => {
      const limitedReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          maxAttempts: 2,
          initialDelay: 50,
        },
      });

      const errorHandler = jest.fn();
      limitedReconnectManager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = limitedReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Trigger multiple closes to exhaust retries
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        mockWs.triggerClose(1006);
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
      }

      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          message: expect.stringContaining('Max reconnection attempts'),
        })
      );
    });

    it('should use exponential backoff for reconnection', async () => {
      const manager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          initialDelay: 100,
          backoffMultiplier: 2,
        },
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const startTime = Date.now();
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 150));

      const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;

      expect(elapsed).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(100);
    });
  });

  describe('event handlers', () => {
    it('should call onOpen handler', async () => {
      const openHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onOpen: openHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(openHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onError handler', async () => {
      const errorHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerError();
      mockWs.triggerClose();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onClose handler', async () => {
      const closeHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onClose: closeHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(closeHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should update handlers', async () => {
      const handler1 = jest.fn();
      const handler2 = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler1 });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test1');

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler2 });
      mockWs.triggerMessage('test2');

      expect(handler1).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
      expect(handler2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    });
  });

  describe('state management', () => {
    it('should transition through states correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTING);

      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSING);

      await disconnectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
    });

    it('should check connection state correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});

```

```typescript
/**
 * WebSocketManager tests
 */

import { WebSocketManager, WebSocketState } from '../../../src/utils/websocket';
import { WebSocketError, TimeoutError } from '../../../src/utils/errors';

// Mock WebSocket
class MockWebSocket {
  public static CONNECTING = 0;
  public static OPEN = 1;
  public static CLOSING = 2;
  public static CLOSED = 3;

  public readyState = MockWebSocket.CONNECTING;
  public onopen: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onmessage: ((event: MessageEvent) => void) | null = null;
  public onerror: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onclose: ((event: CloseEvent) => void) | null = null;

  constructor(
    public url: string,
    public protocols?: string | string[]
  ) {}

  send = jest.fn();
  close = jest.fn((code?: number, reason?: string) => {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(
        new CloseEvent('close', {
          code: code ?? 1000,
          reason: reason ?? '',
        }) as any
      );
    }
  });

  // Test helpers
  triggerOpen() {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.OPEN;
    if (this.onopen) {
      this.onopen(new Event('open'));
    }
  }

  triggerMessage(data: string) {
    if (this.onmessage) {
      this.onmessage(new MessageEvent('message', { data }));
    }
  }

  triggerError() {
    if (this.onerror) {
      this.onerror(new Event('error'));
    }
  }

  triggerClose(code = 1000, reason = '') {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(new CloseEvent('close', { code, reason }) as any);
    }
  }
}

describe('WebSocketManager', () => {
  let manager: WebSocketManager;
  let mockWs: MockWebSocket;

  beforeEach(() => {
    // Mock global WebSocket
    (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
      mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
      // Automatically trigger open after a microtask to simulate async connection
      Promise.resolve().then(() => {
        if (mockWs.readyState === MockWebSocket.CONNECTING) {
          mockWs.triggerOpen();
        }
      });
      return mockWs;
    });

    manager = new WebSocketManager({
      url: 'wss://test.example.com',
      connectionTimeout: 1000,
    });
  });

  afterEach(() => {
    jest.clearAllMocks();
  });

  describe('initialization', () => {
    it('should create manager with options', () => {
      expect(manager).toBeInstanceOf(WebSocketManager);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should not be connected initially', () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('connection', () => {
    it('should connect to WebSocket', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);
    });

    it('should create WebSocket with correct URL', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(mockWs.url).toBe('wss://test.example.com');
    });

    it('should pass protocols to WebSocket', async () => {
      const managerWithProtocols = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        protocols: ['protocol1', 'protocol2'],
      });

      await managerWithProtocols.connect();

      expect(mockWs.protocols).toEqual(['protocol1', 'protocol2']);
    });

    it('should timeout if connection takes too long', async () => {
      const shortTimeoutManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        connectionTimeout: 100,
      });

      await expect(shortTimeoutManager.connect()).rejects.toThrow(TimeoutError);
    });

    it('should not connect twice', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      const wsConstructorCalls = ((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length;

      await manager.connect();

      expect(((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length).toBe(wsConstructorCalls);
    });

    it('should handle connection errors', async () => {
      // Override the auto-open behavior for this test
      (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
        mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
        Promise.resolve().then(() => {
          mockWs.triggerError();
          mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Connection failed');
        });
        return mockWs;
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe('message handling', () => {
    it('should receive messages through handler', async () => {
      const messageHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: messageHandler,
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test message');

      expect(messageHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          data: 'test message',
        })
      );
    });

    it('should handle multiple messages', async () => {
      const messages: string[] = [];

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: (event) => messages.push(event.data),
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('message1');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message2');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message3');

      expect(messages).toEqual(['message1', 'message2', 'message3']);
    });
  });

  describe('sending data', () => {
    it('should send string data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      manager.send('test data');

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith('test data');
    });

    it('should send ArrayBuffer data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(8);
      manager.send(buffer);

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith(buffer);
    });

    it('should throw error when sending while disconnected', () => {
      expect(() => manager.send('test')).toThrow(WebSocketError);
    });
  });

  describe('disconnection', () => {
    it('should disconnect gracefully', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should disconnect with custom code and reason', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect(1001, 'Going away');

      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith(1001, 'Going away');
    });

    it('should handle disconnect when not connected', async () => {
      await expect(manager.disconnect()).resolves.not.toThrow();
    });

    it('should timeout disconnect if it takes too long', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Override close to not trigger event
      mockWs.close = jest.fn();

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();

      // Should resolve after timeout
      await expect(disconnectPromise).resolves.not.toThrow();
    }, 10000);
  });

  describe('reconnection', () => {
    it('should attempt reconnection on unexpected close', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      // Simulate unexpected close
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Abnormal closure');

      // Wait for reconnection attempt
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.RECONNECTING);
    });

    it('should not reconnect if disabled', async () => {
      const noReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: { enabled: false },
      });

      const connectPromise = noReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(noReconnectManager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should stop reconnecting after max attempts', async () => {
      const limitedReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          maxAttempts: 2,
          initialDelay: 50,
        },
      });

      const errorHandler = jest.fn();
      limitedReconnectManager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = limitedReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Trigger multiple closes to exhaust retries
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        mockWs.triggerClose(1006);
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
      }

      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          message: expect.stringContaining('Max reconnection attempts'),
        })
      );
    });

    it('should use exponential backoff for reconnection', async () => {
      const manager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          initialDelay: 100,
          backoffMultiplier: 2,
        },
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const startTime = Date.now();
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 150));

      const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;

      expect(elapsed).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(100);
    });
  });

  describe('event handlers', () => {
    it('should call onOpen handler', async () => {
      const openHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onOpen: openHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(openHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onError handler', async () => {
      const errorHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerError();
      mockWs.triggerClose();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onClose handler', async () => {
      const closeHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onClose: closeHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(closeHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should update handlers', async () => {
      const handler1 = jest.fn();
      const handler2 = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler1 });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test1');

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler2 });
      mockWs.triggerMessage('test2');

      expect(handler1).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
      expect(handler2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    });
  });

  describe('state management', () => {
    it('should transition through states correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTING);

      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSING);

      await disconnectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
    });

    it('should check connection state correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});

```typescript
/**
 * WebSocketManager tests
 */

import { WebSocketManager, WebSocketState } from '../../../src/utils/websocket';
import { WebSocketError, TimeoutError } from '../../../src/utils/errors';

// Mock WebSocket
class MockWebSocket {
  public static CONNECTING = 0;
  public static OPEN = 1;
  public static CLOSING = 2;
  public static CLOSED = 3;

  public readyState = MockWebSocket.CONNECTING;
  public onopen: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onmessage: ((event: MessageEvent) => void) | null = null;
  public onerror: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onclose: ((event: CloseEvent) => void) | null = null;

  constructor(
    public url: string,
    public protocols?: string | string[]
  ) {}

  send = jest.fn();
  close = jest.fn((code?: number, reason?: string) => {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(
        new CloseEvent('close', {
          code: code ?? 1000,
          reason: reason ?? '',
        }) as any
      );
    }
  });

  // Test helpers
  triggerOpen() {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.OPEN;
    if (this.onopen) {
      this.onopen(new Event('open'));
    }
  }

  triggerMessage(data: string) {
    if (this.onmessage) {
      this.onmessage(new MessageEvent('message', { data }));
    }
  }

  triggerError() {
    if (this.onerror) {
      this.onerror(new Event('error'));
    }
  }

  triggerClose(code = 1000, reason = '') {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(new CloseEvent('close', { code, reason }) as any);
    }
  }
}

      await expect(shortTimeoutManager.connect()).rejects.toThrow(TimeoutError);

      await manager.connect();

      expect(((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length).toBe(wsConstructorCalls);
    });

    it('should handle connection errors', async () => {
      // Override the auto-open behavior for this test
      (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
        mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
        Promise.resolve().then(() => {
          mockWs.triggerError();
          mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Connection failed');
        });
        return mockWs;
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe('message handling', () => {
    it('should receive messages through handler', async () => {
      const messageHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: messageHandler,
      });

      await manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test message');

      expect(messageHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          data: 'test message',
        })
      );
    });

    it('should handle multiple messages', async () => {
      const messages: string[] = [];

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: (event) => messages.push(event.data),
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('message1');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message2');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message3');

      expect(messages).toEqual(['message1', 'message2', 'message3']);
    });
  });

  describe('sending data', () => {
    it('should send string data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      manager.send('test data');

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith('test data');
    });

    it('should send ArrayBuffer data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(8);
      manager.send(buffer);

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith(buffer);
    });

    it('should throw error when sending while disconnected', () => {
      expect(() => manager.send('test')).toThrow(WebSocketError);
    });
  });

  describe('disconnection', () => {
    it('should disconnect gracefully', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should disconnect with custom code and reason', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect(1001, 'Going away');

      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith(1001, 'Going away');
    });

    it('should handle disconnect when not connected', async () => {
      await expect(manager.disconnect()).resolves.not.toThrow();
    });

    it('should timeout disconnect if it takes too long', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Override close to not trigger event
      mockWs.close = jest.fn();

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();

      // Should resolve after timeout
      await expect(disconnectPromise).resolves.not.toThrow();
    }, 10000);
  });

  describe('reconnection', () => {
    it('should attempt reconnection on unexpected close', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      // Simulate unexpected close
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Abnormal closure');

      // Wait for reconnection attempt
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.RECONNECTING);
    });

    it('should not reconnect if disabled', async () => {
      const noReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: { enabled: false },
      });

      const connectPromise = noReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(noReconnectManager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should stop reconnecting after max attempts', async () => {
      const limitedReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          maxAttempts: 2,
          initialDelay: 50,
        },
      });

      const errorHandler = jest.fn();
      limitedReconnectManager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = limitedReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Trigger multiple closes to exhaust retries
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        mockWs.triggerClose(1006);
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
      }

      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          message: expect.stringContaining('Max reconnection attempts'),
        })
      );
    });

    it('should use exponential backoff for reconnection', async () => {
      const manager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          initialDelay: 100,
          backoffMultiplier: 2,
        },
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const startTime = Date.now();
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 150));

      const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;

      expect(elapsed).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(100);
    });
  });

  describe('event handlers', () => {
    it('should call onOpen handler', async () => {
      const openHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onOpen: openHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(openHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onError handler', async () => {
      const errorHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerError();
      mockWs.triggerClose();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onClose handler', async () => {
      const closeHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onClose: closeHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(closeHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should update handlers', async () => {
      const handler1 = jest.fn();
      const handler2 = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler1 });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test1');

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler2 });
      mockWs.triggerMessage('test2');

      expect(handler1).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
      expect(handler2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    });
  });

  describe('state management', () => {
    it('should transition through states correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTING);

      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSING);

      await disconnectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
    });

    it('should check connection state correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});

```

```typescript
/**
 * WebSocketManager tests
 */

import { WebSocketManager, WebSocketState } from '../../../src/utils/websocket';
import { WebSocketError, TimeoutError } from '../../../src/utils/errors';

// Mock WebSocket
class MockWebSocket {
  public static CONNECTING = 0;
  public static OPEN = 1;
  public static CLOSING = 2;
  public static CLOSED = 3;

  public readyState = MockWebSocket.CONNECTING;
  public onopen: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onmessage: ((event: MessageEvent) => void) | null = null;
  public onerror: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onclose: ((event: CloseEvent) => void) | null = null;

  constructor(
    public url: string,
    public protocols?: string | string[]
  ) {}

  send = jest.fn();
  close = jest.fn((code?: number, reason?: string) => {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(
        new CloseEvent('close', {
          code: code ?? 1000,
          reason: reason ?? '',
        }) as any
      );
    }
  });

  // Test helpers
  triggerOpen() {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.OPEN;
    if (this.onopen) {
      this.onopen(new Event('open'));
    }
  }

  triggerMessage(data: string) {
    if (this.onmessage) {
      this.onmessage(new MessageEvent('message', { data }));
    }
  }

  triggerError() {
    if (this.onerror) {
      this.onerror(new Event('error'));
    }
  }

  triggerClose(code = 1000, reason = '') {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(new CloseEvent('close', { code, reason }) as any);
    }
  }
}

describe('WebSocketManager', () => {
  let manager: WebSocketManager;
  let mockWs: MockWebSocket;

  beforeEach(() => {
    // Mock global WebSocket
    (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
      mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
      // Automatically trigger open after a microtask to simulate async connection
      Promise.resolve().then(() => {
        if (mockWs.readyState === MockWebSocket.CONNECTING) {
          mockWs.triggerOpen();
        }
      });
      return mockWs;
    });

    manager = new WebSocketManager({
      url: 'wss://test.example.com',
      connectionTimeout: 1000,
    });
  });

  afterEach(() => {
    jest.clearAllMocks();
  });

  describe('initialization', () => {
    it('should create manager with options', () => {
      expect(manager).toBeInstanceOf(WebSocketManager);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should not be connected initially', () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('connection', () => {
    it('should connect to WebSocket', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);
    });

    it('should create WebSocket with correct URL', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(mockWs.url).toBe('wss://test.example.com');
    });

    it('should pass protocols to WebSocket', async () => {
      const managerWithProtocols = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        protocols: ['protocol1', 'protocol2'],
      });

      await managerWithProtocols.connect();

      expect(mockWs.protocols).toEqual(['protocol1', 'protocol2']);
    });

    it('should timeout if connection takes too long', async () => {
      const shortTimeoutManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        connectionTimeout: 100,
      });

      await expect(shortTimeoutManager.connect()).rejects.toThrow(TimeoutError);
    });

    it('should not connect twice', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      const wsConstructorCalls = ((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length;

      await manager.connect();

      expect(((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length).toBe(wsConstructorCalls);
    });

    it('should handle connection errors', async () => {
      // Override the auto-open behavior for this test
      (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
        mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
        Promise.resolve().then(() => {
          mockWs.triggerError();
          mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Connection failed');
        });
        return mockWs;
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe('message handling', () => {
    it('should receive messages through handler', async () => {
      const messageHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: messageHandler,
      });

      await manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test message');

      expect(messageHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          data: 'test message',
        })
      );
    });

    it('should handle multiple messages', async () => {
      const messages: string[] = [];

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: (event) => messages.push(event.data),
      });

      await manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerMessage('message1');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message2');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message3');

      expect(messages).toEqual(['message1', 'message2', 'message3']);
    });
  });

  describe('sending data', () => {
    it('should send string data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      manager.send('test data');

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith('test data');
    });

    it('should send ArrayBuffer data', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(8);
      manager.send(buffer);

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith(buffer);
    });

    it('should throw error when sending while disconnected', () => {
      expect(() => manager.send('test')).toThrow(WebSocketError);
    });
  });

  describe('disconnection', () => {
    it('should disconnect gracefully', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should disconnect with custom code and reason', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect(1001, 'Going away');

      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith(1001, 'Going away');
    });

    it('should handle disconnect when not connected', async () => {
      await expect(manager.disconnect()).resolves.not.toThrow();
    });

    it('should timeout disconnect if it takes too long', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Override close to not trigger event
      mockWs.close = jest.fn();

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();

      // Should resolve after timeout
      await expect(disconnectPromise).resolves.not.toThrow();
    }, 10000);
  });

  describe('reconnection', () => {
    it('should attempt reconnection on unexpected close', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      // Simulate unexpected close
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Abnormal closure');

      // Wait for reconnection attempt
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.RECONNECTING);
    });

    it('should not reconnect if disabled', async () => {
      const noReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: { enabled: false },
      });

      const connectPromise = noReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(noReconnectManager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should stop reconnecting after max attempts', async () => {
      const limitedReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          maxAttempts: 2,
          initialDelay: 50,
        },
      });

      const errorHandler = jest.fn();
      limitedReconnectManager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = limitedReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Trigger multiple closes to exhaust retries
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        mockWs.triggerClose(1006);
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
      }

      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          message: expect.stringContaining('Max reconnection attempts'),
        })
      );
    });

    it('should use exponential backoff for reconnection', async () => {
      const manager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          initialDelay: 100,
          backoffMultiplier: 2,
        },
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const startTime = Date.now();
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 150));

      const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;

      expect(elapsed).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(100);
    });
  });

  describe('event handlers', () => {
    it('should call onOpen handler', async () => {
      const openHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onOpen: openHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(openHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onError handler', async () => {
      const errorHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerError();
      mockWs.triggerClose();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onClose handler', async () => {
      const closeHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onClose: closeHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(closeHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should update handlers', async () => {
      const handler1 = jest.fn();
      const handler2 = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler1 });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test1');

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler2 });
      mockWs.triggerMessage('test2');

      expect(handler1).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
      expect(handler2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    });
  });

  describe('state management', () => {
    it('should transition through states correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTING);

      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSING);

      await disconnectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
    });

    it('should check connection state correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});

```

```typescript
/**
 * WebSocketManager tests
 */

import { WebSocketManager, WebSocketState } from '../../../src/utils/websocket';
import { WebSocketError, TimeoutError } from '../../../src/utils/errors';

// Mock WebSocket
class MockWebSocket {
  public static CONNECTING = 0;
  public static OPEN = 1;
  public static CLOSING = 2;
  public static CLOSED = 3;

  public readyState = MockWebSocket.CONNECTING;
  public onopen: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onmessage: ((event: MessageEvent) => void) | null = null;
  public onerror: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onclose: ((event: CloseEvent) => void) | null = null;

  constructor(
    public url: string,
    public protocols?: string | string[]
  ) {}

  send = jest.fn();
  close = jest.fn((code?: number, reason?: string) => {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(
        new CloseEvent('close', {
          code: code ?? 1000,
          reason: reason ?? '',
        }) as any
      );
    }
  });

  // Test helpers
  triggerOpen() {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.OPEN;
    if (this.onopen) {
      this.onopen(new Event('open'));
    }
  }

  triggerMessage(data: string) {
    if (this.onmessage) {
      this.onmessage(new MessageEvent('message', { data }));
    }
  }

  triggerError() {
    if (this.onerror) {
      this.onerror(new Event('error'));
    }
  }

  triggerClose(code = 1000, reason = '') {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(new CloseEvent('close', { code, reason }) as any);
    }
  }
}

describe('WebSocketManager', () => {
  let manager: WebSocketManager;
  let mockWs: MockWebSocket;

  beforeEach(() => {

    (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {

      url: 'wss://test.example.com',
      connectionTimeout: 1000,
    });
  });

  afterEach(() => {
    jest.clearAllMocks();
  });

      await managerWithProtocols.connect();

      expect(mockWs.protocols).toEqual(['protocol1', 'protocol2']);
    });

    it('should timeout if connection takes too long', async () => {
      const shortTimeoutManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        connectionTimeout: 100,
      });

      await expect(shortTimeoutManager.connect()).rejects.toThrow(TimeoutError);
    });

    it('should not connect twice', async () => {

      const wsConstructorCalls = ((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length;

      await manager.connect();

      expect(((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length).toBe(wsConstructorCalls);
    });

    it('should handle connection errors', async () => {
      // Override the auto-open behavior for this test
      (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
        mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
        Promise.resolve().then(() => {
          mockWs.triggerError();
          mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Connection failed');
        });
        return mockWs;
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe('message handling', () => {
    it('should receive messages through handler', async () => {
      const messageHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: messageHandler,
      });

      await manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test message');

      expect(messageHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          data: 'test message',
        })
      );
    });

    it('should handle multiple messages', async () => {
      const messages: string[] = [];

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: (event) => messages.push(event.data),
      });

      await manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerMessage('message1');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message2');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message3');

      expect(messages).toEqual(['message1', 'message2', 'message3']);
    });
  });

  describe('sending data', () => {
    it('should send string data', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      manager.send('test data');

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith('test data');
    });

    it('should send ArrayBuffer data', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(8);
      manager.send(buffer);

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith(buffer);
    });

    it('should throw error when sending while disconnected', () => {
      expect(() => manager.send('test')).toThrow(WebSocketError);
    });
  });

  describe('disconnection', () => {
    it('should disconnect gracefully', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should disconnect with custom code and reason', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect(1001, 'Going away');

      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith(1001, 'Going away');
    });

    it('should handle disconnect when not connected', async () => {
      await expect(manager.disconnect()).resolves.not.toThrow();
    });

    it('should timeout disconnect if it takes too long', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Override close to not trigger event
      mockWs.close = jest.fn();

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();

      // Should resolve after timeout
      await expect(disconnectPromise).resolves.not.toThrow();
    }, 10000);
  });

  describe('reconnection', () => {
    it('should attempt reconnection on unexpected close', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      // Simulate unexpected close
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Abnormal closure');

      // Wait for reconnection attempt
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.RECONNECTING);
    });

    it('should not reconnect if disabled', async () => {
      const noReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: { enabled: false },
      });

      const connectPromise = noReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(noReconnectManager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should stop reconnecting after max attempts', async () => {
      const limitedReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          maxAttempts: 2,
          initialDelay: 50,
        },
      });

      const errorHandler = jest.fn();
      limitedReconnectManager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = limitedReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Trigger multiple closes to exhaust retries
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        mockWs.triggerClose(1006);
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
      }

      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          message: expect.stringContaining('Max reconnection attempts'),
        })
      );
    });

    it('should use exponential backoff for reconnection', async () => {
      const manager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          initialDelay: 100,
          backoffMultiplier: 2,
        },
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const startTime = Date.now();
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 150));

      const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;

      expect(elapsed).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(100);
    });
  });

  describe('event handlers', () => {
    it('should call onOpen handler', async () => {
      const openHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onOpen: openHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(openHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onError handler', async () => {
      const errorHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerError();
      mockWs.triggerClose();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onClose handler', async () => {
      const closeHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onClose: closeHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(closeHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should update handlers', async () => {
      const handler1 = jest.fn();
      const handler2 = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler1 });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test1');

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler2 });
      mockWs.triggerMessage('test2');

      expect(handler1).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
      expect(handler2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    });
  });

  describe('state management', () => {
    it('should transition through states correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTING);

      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSING);

      await disconnectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
    });

    it('should check connection state correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});

```

```typescript
/**
 * WebSocketManager tests
 */

import { WebSocketManager, WebSocketState } from '../../../src/utils/websocket';
import { WebSocketError, TimeoutError } from '../../../src/utils/errors';

// Mock WebSocket
class MockWebSocket {
  public static CONNECTING = 0;
  public static OPEN = 1;
  public static CLOSING = 2;
  public static CLOSED = 3;

  public readyState = MockWebSocket.CONNECTING;
  public onopen: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onmessage: ((event: MessageEvent) => void) | null = null;
  public onerror: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onclose: ((event: CloseEvent) => void) | null = null;

  constructor(
    public url: string,
    public protocols?: string | string[]
  ) {}

  send = jest.fn();
  close = jest.fn((code?: number, reason?: string) => {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(
        new CloseEvent('close', {
          code: code ?? 1000,
          reason: reason ?? '',
        }) as any
      );
    }
  });

  // Test helpers
  triggerOpen() {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.OPEN;
    if (this.onopen) {
      this.onopen(new Event('open'));
    }
  }

  triggerMessage(data: string) {
    if (this.onmessage) {
      this.onmessage(new MessageEvent('message', { data }));
    }
  }

  triggerError() {
    if (this.onerror) {
      this.onerror(new Event('error'));
    }
  }

  triggerClose(code = 1000, reason = '') {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(new CloseEvent('close', { code, reason }) as any);
    }
  }
}

describe('WebSocketManager', () => {
  let manager: WebSocketManager;
  let mockWs: MockWebSocket;

  beforeEach(() => {
    // Mock global WebSocket
    (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
      mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
      // Automatically trigger open after a microtask to simulate async connection
      Promise.resolve().then(() => {
        if (mockWs.readyState === MockWebSocket.CONNECTING) {
          mockWs.triggerOpen();
        }
      });
      return mockWs;
    });

    manager = new WebSocketManager({
      url: 'wss://test.example.com',
      connectionTimeout: 1000,
    });
  });

  afterEach(() => {
    jest.clearAllMocks();
  });

  describe('initialization', () => {
    it('should create manager with options', () => {
      expect(manager).toBeInstanceOf(WebSocketManager);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should not be connected initially', () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('connection', () => {
    it('should connect to WebSocket', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);
    });

    it('should create WebSocket with correct URL', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      expect(mockWs.url).toBe('wss://test.example.com');
    });

    it('should pass protocols to WebSocket', async () => {
      const managerWithProtocols = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        protocols: ['protocol1', 'protocol2'],
      });

      await managerWithProtocols.connect();

      expect(mockWs.protocols).toEqual(['protocol1', 'protocol2']);
    });

    it('should timeout if connection takes too long', async () => {
      const shortTimeoutManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        connectionTimeout: 100,
      });

      await expect(shortTimeoutManager.connect()).rejects.toThrow(TimeoutError);
    });

    it('should not connect twice', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      const wsConstructorCalls = ((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length;

      await manager.connect();

      expect(((global as any).WebSocket as jest.Mock).mock.calls.length).toBe(wsConstructorCalls);
    });

    it('should handle connection errors', async () => {
      // Override the auto-open behavior for this test
      (global as any).WebSocket = jest.fn((url: string, protocols?: string | string[]) => {
        mockWs = new MockWebSocket(url, protocols);
        Promise.resolve().then(() => {
          mockWs.triggerError();
          mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Connection failed');
        });
        return mockWs;
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe('message handling', () => {
    it('should receive messages through handler', async () => {
      const messageHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: messageHandler,
      });

      await manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test message');

      expect(messageHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          data: 'test message',
        })
      );
    });

    it('should handle multiple messages', async () => {
      const messages: string[] = [];

      manager.setHandlers({
        onMessage: (event) => messages.push(event.data),
      });

      await manager.connect();

      mockWs.triggerMessage('message1');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message2');
      mockWs.triggerMessage('message3');

      expect(messages).toEqual(['message1', 'message2', 'message3']);
    });
  });

  describe('sending data', () => {
    it('should send string data', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      manager.send('test data');

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith('test data');
    });

    it('should send ArrayBuffer data', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      const buffer = new ArrayBuffer(8);
      manager.send(buffer);

      expect(mockWs.send).toHaveBeenCalledWith(buffer);
    });

    it('should throw error when sending while disconnected', () => {
      expect(() => manager.send('test')).toThrow(WebSocketError);
    });
  });

  describe('disconnection', () => {
    it('should disconnect gracefully', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should disconnect with custom code and reason', async () => {
      await manager.connect();

      await manager.disconnect(1001, 'Going away');

      expect(mockWs.close).toHaveBeenCalledWith(1001, 'Going away');
    });

    it('should handle disconnect when not connected', async () => {
      await expect(manager.disconnect()).resolves.not.toThrow();
    });

    it('should timeout disconnect if it takes too long', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Override close to not trigger event
      mockWs.close = jest.fn();

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();

      // Should resolve after timeout
      await expect(disconnectPromise).resolves.not.toThrow();
    }, 10000);
  });

  describe('reconnection', () => {
    it('should attempt reconnection on unexpected close', async () => {
      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      // Simulate unexpected close
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006, 'Abnormal closure');

      // Wait for reconnection attempt
      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.RECONNECTING);
    });

    it('should not reconnect if disabled', async () => {
      const noReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: { enabled: false },
      });

      const connectPromise = noReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

      expect(noReconnectManager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);
    });

    it('should stop reconnecting after max attempts', async () => {
      const limitedReconnectManager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          maxAttempts: 2,
          initialDelay: 50,
        },
      });

      const errorHandler = jest.fn();
      limitedReconnectManager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = limitedReconnectManager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      // Trigger multiple closes to exhaust retries
      for (let i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        mockWs.triggerClose(1006);
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
      }

      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalledWith(
        expect.objectContaining({
          message: expect.stringContaining('Max reconnection attempts'),
        })
      );
    });

    it('should use exponential backoff for reconnection', async () => {
      const manager = new WebSocketManager({
        url: 'wss://test.example.com',
        reconnection: {
          enabled: true,
          initialDelay: 100,
          backoffMultiplier: 2,
        },
      });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      const startTime = Date.now();
      mockWs.triggerClose(1006);

      await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 150));

      const elapsed = Date.now() - startTime;

      expect(elapsed).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(100);
    });
  });

  describe('event handlers', () => {
    it('should call onOpen handler', async () => {
      const openHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onOpen: openHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(openHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onError handler', async () => {
      const errorHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onError: errorHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerError();
      mockWs.triggerClose();

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
      expect(errorHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should call onClose handler', async () => {
      const closeHandler = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onClose: closeHandler });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(closeHandler).toHaveBeenCalled();
    });

    it('should update handlers', async () => {
      const handler1 = jest.fn();
      const handler2 = jest.fn();

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler1 });

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      mockWs.triggerMessage('test1');

      manager.setHandlers({ onMessage: handler2 });
      mockWs.triggerMessage('test2');

      expect(handler1).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
      expect(handler2).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
    });
  });

  describe('state management', () => {
    it('should transition through states correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.DISCONNECTED);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTING);

      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CONNECTED);

      const disconnectPromise = manager.disconnect();
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSING);

      await disconnectPromise;
      expect(manager.getState()).toBe(WebSocketState.CLOSED);
    });

    it('should check connection state correctly', async () => {
      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);

      const connectPromise = manager.connect();
      mockWs.triggerOpen();
      await connectPromise;

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(true);

      await manager.disconnect();

      expect(manager.isConnected()).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});

```

```typescript
/**

import { WebSocketManager, WebSocketState } from '../../../src/utils/websocket';
import { WebSocketError, TimeoutError } from '../../../src/utils/errors';

// Mock WebSocket
class MockWebSocket {
  public static CONNECTING = 0;
  public static OPEN = 1;
  public static CLOSING = 2;
  public static CLOSED = 3;

  public readyState = MockWebSocket.CONNECTING;
  public onopen: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onmessage: ((event: MessageEvent) => void) | null = null;
  public onerror: ((event: Event) => void) | null = null;
  public onclose: ((event: CloseEvent) => void) | null = null;

  constructor(
    public url: string,
    public protocols?: string | string[]
  ) {}

  send = jest.fn();
  close = jest.fn((code?: number, reason?: string) => {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(
        new CloseEvent('close', {
          code: code ?? 1000,
          reason: reason ?? '',
        }) as any
      );
    }
  });

  // Test helpers
  triggerOpen() {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.OPEN;
    if (this.onopen) {
      this.onopen(new Event('open'));
    }
  }

  triggerMessage(data: string) {

      this.onmessage(new MessageEvent('message', { data }));
    }
  }

  triggerError() {
    if (this.onerror) {
      this.onerror(new Event('error'));
    }
  }

  triggerClose(code = 1000, reason = '') {
    this.readyState = MockWebSocket.CLOSED;
    if (this.onclose) {
      this.onclose(new CloseEvent('close', { code, reason }) as any);
    }
  }
}

        });

      });

      await expect(connectPromise).rejects.toThrow();
    });
  });

  describe('message handling', () => {

      });

      );
    });

    it('should handle multiple messages', async () => {
